Du bist ein erfahrener Java-Reviewer.
    Architektur: 4-Layer (Eric Evans).
    Aufgabe: Finde folgende Smells: Duplication: duplizierte Codestücke die mehrmals vorkommen und eingespart werden könnten. Gib hierbei sowohl die duplizierte als auch die originale Zeile an. Bei längeren kopierten Abschnitten gib auch hier die Zeilen als Bereich an.  negative conditionals: Es handelt sich hierbei um negativ oder doppelt negativ formulierte Bedingungen und Variablen. Einfach formulierte Negierungen in if-Anweisungen sind okay solange sie verständlich sind.  dead code: Nicht genutzer Code. Klassen, Methoden und Variablen die nie aufgerufen werden.  layer violation: Es wurde sich nicht an die Package und Ebenenstruktur gehalten. Zum Beispiel Zugriff auf den Domainlayer eines anderen Pakets. missplaced resonsibility: Dieser Code ist an der falschen Stelle. Entweder gehört er in ein anderes Package oder in einen andere Schicht oder in eine andere Klasse. Shared persistency: Zugriff auf die Repositories der Domainschicht eines anderen Packages. Anemic Entity: Domain Entities in der Domainschicht die nur über Getter oder Setter verfügen aber sonst keine Funktionen. Ausgenommen sind Repositories. Für diesen Smell brauchst du keinen Zeilenangabe, da er für die gesamte Klasse gilt. Schreib einfach nur einmal -Anemic Entity- sonst zu der enstrechenden Datei.
    Regeln:
    1. Begründe kurz jeden Fund.
    4. Gruppiere nach Datei (mit Pfad). 
    2. Format unter der Datei je Smell: [Dateiname (ohne Pfad)] [Zeile(n) X]: [Smell] [Nur bei Duplizierung: die original Zeile(n)] : [Begründung].
    3. Keine Code-Wiederholung, nur Referenzen.
    5. Wenn fertig, schreibe "ENDE".

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.AddressLocationType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PostalCodeType;

import java.util.Objects;

public class AddressLocation implements AddressLocationType {
    @JsonProperty("street")
    private final String street;
    @JsonProperty("city")
    private final String city;
    @JsonProperty("postalCode")
    private final PostalCodeType postalCode;

    @JsonCreator
    private AddressLocation(@JsonProperty("street") String street, @JsonProperty("city") String city, @JsonProperty("postalCode") PostalCode postalCode) {
        if (street == null || street.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Street cannot be null or empty");
        }
        if (city == null || city.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("City cannot be null or empty");
        }
        if (postalCode == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Postal code cannot be null");
        }
        this.street = street.trim();
        this.city = city.trim();
        this.postalCode = postalCode;
    }

    public static AddressLocation of(String street, String city, PostalCodeType postalCode) {
        return new AddressLocation(street, city, (PostalCode) postalCode);
    }

    public static AddressLocation of(String street, String city, String postalCodeString) {
        return new AddressLocation(street, city, PostalCode.of(postalCodeString));
    }

    public String getStreet() {
        return street;
    }

    public String getCity() {
        return city;
    }

    public PostalCodeType getPostalCode() {
        return postalCode;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        AddressLocation that = (AddressLocation) o;
        return Objects.equals(street, that.street) &&
               Objects.equals(city, that.city) &&
               Objects.equals(postalCode, that.postalCode);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(street, city, postalCode);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return street + ", " + city + " " + postalCode;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.CurrencyType;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.math.RoundingMode;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;

public class Currency implements CurrencyType {
    private final BigDecimal amount;
    @JsonProperty("currencyUnit")
    private final String currencyCode;
    private static final Set<String> ALLOWED_CURRENCIES = Set.of("EUR", "CHF");

    @JsonCreator
    private Currency(@JsonProperty("quantity") Float quantity, @JsonProperty("currencyUnit") String currencyCode) {
        this(quantity != null ? BigDecimal.valueOf(quantity) : null, currencyCode);
    }
    
    private Currency(BigDecimal amount, String currencyCode) {
        if (amount == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Amount cannot be null");
        }
        if (amount.compareTo(BigDecimal.ZERO) < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Amount cannot be negative");
        }
        if (currencyCode == null || currencyCode.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Currency code cannot be null or empty");
        }
        String upperCode = currencyCode.toUpperCase();
        if (!ALLOWED_CURRENCIES.contains(upperCode)) {
            throw new ShopException("Currency code must be EUR or CHF");
        }
        this.amount = amount.setScale(2, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
        this.currencyCode = upperCode;
    }

    public static Currency of(Float quantity, String currencyUnit) {
        if (quantity == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Quantity cannot be null");
        }
        return new Currency(BigDecimal.valueOf(quantity), currencyUnit);
    }

    public static Currency of(double amount, String currencyCode) {
        return new Currency(BigDecimal.valueOf(amount), currencyCode);
    }

    public static Currency of(BigDecimal amount, String currencyCode) {
        return new Currency(amount, currencyCode);
    }

    @Override
    @JsonProperty("quantity")
    public Float getQuantity() {
        return amount.floatValue();
    }

    @Override
    public String getCurrencyUnit() {
        return currencyCode;
    }

    @Override
    public CurrencyType add(CurrencyType otherCurrency) {
        if (otherCurrency == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Other currency cannot be null");
        }
        if (!this.currencyCode.equals(otherCurrency.getCurrencyUnit())) {
            throw new ShopException("Cannot add different currencies");
        }
        BigDecimal newAmount = this.amount.add(BigDecimal.valueOf(otherCurrency.getQuantity()));
        return new Currency(newAmount, this.currencyCode);
    }

    @Override
    public CurrencyType subtract(CurrencyType otherCurrency) {
        if (otherCurrency == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Other currency cannot be null");
        }
        if (!this.currencyCode.equals(otherCurrency.getCurrencyUnit())) {
            throw new ShopException("Cannot subtract different currencies");
        }
        BigDecimal otherAmount = BigDecimal.valueOf(otherCurrency.getQuantity());
        if (otherAmount.compareTo(this.amount) > 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Cannot subtract larger amount");
        }
        BigDecimal newAmount = this.amount.subtract(otherAmount);
        return new Currency(newAmount, this.currencyCode);
    }

    @Override
    public CurrencyType multiplyBy(int factor) {
        if (factor < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Factor cannot be negative");
        }
        BigDecimal newAmount = this.amount.multiply(BigDecimal.valueOf(factor));
        return new Currency(newAmount, this.currencyCode);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean largerThan(CurrencyType otherCurrency) {
        if (otherCurrency == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Other currency cannot be null");
        }
        if (!this.currencyCode.equals(otherCurrency.getCurrencyUnit())) {
            throw new ShopException("Cannot compare different currencies");
        }
        return this.amount.compareTo(BigDecimal.valueOf(otherCurrency.getQuantity())) > 0;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        Currency currency = (Currency) o;
        return amount.compareTo(currency.amount) == 0 && 
               Objects.equals(currencyCode, currency.currencyCode);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(amount, currencyCode);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return amount.toPlainString() + " " + currencyCode;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailAddressType;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class EmailAddress implements EmailAddressType {
    @JsonProperty("emailAddressString")
    private final String emailAddressString;
    private static final Set<String> ALLOWED_DOMAINS = Set.of(".de", ".at", ".ch", ".com", ".org");

    @JsonCreator
    private EmailAddress(@JsonProperty("emailAddressString") String emailAddressString) {
        if (emailAddressString == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Email address cannot be null");
        }
        
        validateEmailFormat(emailAddressString);
        this.emailAddressString = emailAddressString;
    }

    private static void validateEmailFormat(String email) {
        // Check for exactly one @ character
        int atCount = 0;
        int atIndex = -1;
        for (int i = 0; i < email.length(); i++) {
            if (email.charAt(i) == '@') {
                atCount++;
                atIndex = i;
            }
        }
        if (atCount != 1) {
            throw new ShopException("Email must contain exactly one @ character");
        }

        String identifier = email.substring(0, atIndex);
        String domain = email.substring(atIndex + 1);

        // Validate identifier
        validateEmailPart(identifier, "Identifier");
        
        // Validate domain
        validateEmailPart(domain, "Domain");
        
        // Check domain ending
        boolean hasValidEnding = false;
        for (String ending : ALLOWED_DOMAINS) {
            if (domain.endsWith(ending)) {
                hasValidEnding = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!hasValidEnding) {
            throw new ShopException("Domain must end with .de, .at, .ch, .com, or .org");
        }
    }

    private static void validateEmailPart(String part, String partName) {
        if (part.isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException(partName + " cannot be empty");
        }
        
        // Check for whitespace
        if (part.contains(" ") || part.contains("\t") || part.contains("\n")) {
            throw new ShopException(partName + " cannot contain whitespace");
        }
        
        // Check for invalid characters (only allow letters, digits, dots, hyphens, underscores)
        for (char c : part.toCharArray()) {
            if (!Character.isLetterOrDigit(c) && c != '.' && c != '-' && c != '_') {
                throw new ShopException(partName + " contains invalid character: " + c);
            }
        }
        
        // Check for at least one alphanumeric character
        boolean hasAlphanumeric = false;
        for (char c : part.toCharArray()) {
            if (Character.isLetterOrDigit(c)) {
                hasAlphanumeric = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!hasAlphanumeric) {
            throw new ShopException(partName + " must contain at least one alphanumeric character");
        }
        
        // Check for consecutive dots
        if (part.contains("..")) {
            throw new ShopException(partName + " cannot contain consecutive dots");
        }
    }

    public static EmailAddress of(String emailAddressString) {
        return new EmailAddress(emailAddressString);
    }

    public String getEmailAddressString() {
        return emailAddressString;
    }

    @Override
    public EmailAddressType sameIdentifyerDifferentDomain(String domainString) {
        if (domainString == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Domain string cannot be null");
        }
        int atIndex = emailAddressString.indexOf('@');
        String identifier = emailAddressString.substring(0, atIndex);
        return EmailAddress.of(identifier + "@" + domainString);
    }

    @Override
    public EmailAddressType sameDomainDifferentIdentifyer(String identifyerString) {
        if (identifyerString == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Identifier string cannot be null");
        }
        int atIndex = emailAddressString.indexOf('@');
        String domain = emailAddressString.substring(atIndex + 1);
        return EmailAddress.of(identifyerString + "@" + domain);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        EmailAddress that = (EmailAddress) o;
        return Objects.equals(emailAddressString, that.emailAddressString);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(emailAddressString);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return emailAddressString;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PostalCodeType;

import java.util.Objects;

public class PostalCode implements PostalCodeType {
    @JsonProperty("postalCodeString")
    private final String postalCodeString;

    @JsonCreator
    private PostalCode(@JsonProperty("postalCodeString") String postalCodeString) {
        if (postalCodeString == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Postal code cannot be null");
        }
        
        // Must contain exactly 5 digits
        if (!postalCodeString.matches("^[0-9]{5}$")) {
            throw new ShopException("Postal code must contain exactly 5 digits");
        }
        
        // Last 4 digits must not be 0000
        if (postalCodeString.endsWith("0000")) {
            throw new ShopException("Last 4 digits of postal code cannot be 0000");
        }
        
        this.postalCodeString = postalCodeString;
    }

    public static PostalCode of(String postalCodeString) {
        return new PostalCode(postalCodeString);
    }

    public String getPostalCodeString() {
        return postalCodeString;
    }

    @Override
    public int distance(PostalCodeType otherPostalCode) {
        if (otherPostalCode == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Other postal code cannot be null");
        }
        
        String other = otherPostalCode.toString();
        if (this.postalCodeString.equals(other)) {
            return 0;
        }
        
        // Find the leftmost position where digits differ
        int leftmostDiffPos = -1;
        for (int i = 0; i <= 4; i++) {
            if (this.postalCodeString.charAt(i) != other.charAt(i)) {
                leftmostDiffPos = i;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if (leftmostDiffPos == -1) {
            return 0; // Should not happen as we already checked equality
        }
        
        // Base distance: 100 * (position from right + 1)
        // Position 0 (leftmost) = 500, position 1 = 400, ..., position 4 (rightmost) = 100
        int baseDistance = 100 * (5 - leftmostDiffPos);
        
        // If the first digit differs (position 0), add additional distance based on digit difference
        if (leftmostDiffPos == 0) {
            int digit1 = Character.getNumericValue(this.postalCodeString.charAt(0));
            int digit2 = Character.getNumericValue(other.charAt(0));
            int diff = Math.abs(digit1 - digit2);
            
            // Handle wrap-around: 0 and 9 are closer than 0 and 5
            if (diff > 5) {
                diff = 10 - diff;
            }
            
            baseDistance += diff * 10;
        }
        
        return baseDistance;
    }

    @Override
    public Integer getFirstDigitPostalCode() {
        return Character.getNumericValue(postalCodeString.charAt(0));
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        PostalCode that = (PostalCode) o;
        return Objects.equals(postalCodeString, that.postalCodeString);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(postalCodeString);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return postalCodeString;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce;

import jakarta.persistence.Column;
import jakarta.persistence.MappedSuperclass;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.ToString;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.UUID;

@MappedSuperclass
@Getter
@EqualsAndHashCode(of = "id")
@ToString(of = "id")
public abstract class GenericId implements Serializable {
    @Column(nullable = false, updatable = false)
    private final UUID id;

    protected GenericId() {
        this( UUID.randomUUID() );
    }

    protected GenericId( UUID id ) {
        this.id = id;
    }
}


--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\Rest\ST2M4_group_e65b9b6a-b74d-481b-b418-a4ed941ec83a\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\GenericIdConverter.java ---
/*
 * Copyright ArchiLab 2025, Cologne University of Applied Sciences, Faculty 10
 */
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce;

import jakarta.persistence.AttributeConverter;

import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.function.Function;


public abstract class GenericIdConverter<T extends GenericId> implements AttributeConverter<T, UUID> {
    private final Function<UUID, T> factory;

    protected GenericIdConverter( Function<UUID, T> factory ) {
        this.factory = factory;
    }

    @Override
    public UUID convertToDatabaseColumn( T attribute ) {
        return attribute == null ? null : attribute.getId();
    }

    @Override
    public T convertToEntityAttribute( UUID dbData ) {
        return dbData == null ? null : factory.apply( dbData );
    }
}

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\Rest\ST2M4_group_e65b9b6a-b74d-481b-b418-a4ed941ec83a\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\order\application\OrderService.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmailAddress;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.Order;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.OrderId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.OrderRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.OrderUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ProductCatalogUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailAddressType;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class OrderService implements OrderUseCases {
    
    private final OrderRepository orderRepository;
    private final UserRepository userRepository;
    private final ProductCatalogUseCases productCatalogUseCases;
    
    @Autowired
    public OrderService(OrderRepository orderRepository, 
                       UserRepository userRepository,
                       ProductCatalogUseCases productCatalogUseCases) {
        this.orderRepository = orderRepository;
        this.userRepository = userRepository;
        this.productCatalogUseCases = productCatalogUseCases;
    }
    
    @Override
    public Map<UUID, Integer> getOrderHistory(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("User email address cannot be null");
        }
        
        String emailString = ((EmailAddress) userEmailAddress).getEmailAddressString();
        User user = userRepository.findByEmailAddress(emailString)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + emailString + " does not exist"));
        
        List<Order> orders = orderRepository.findByUserId(user.getId());
        
        // Aggregate quantities across all orders for each product
        Map<UUID, Integer> orderHistory = new HashMap<>();
        for (Order order : orders) {
            Map<UUID, Integer> orderProducts = order.getOrderAsMap();
            for (Map.Entry<UUID, Integer> entry : orderProducts.entrySet()) {
                orderHistory.merge(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue(), Integer::sum);
            }
        }
        
        return orderHistory;
    }
    
    @Override
    public Integer getOrderQuantiOfProduct(UUID orderId, UUID productId) {
        if (orderId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Order ID cannot be null");
        }
        if (productId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID cannot be null");
        }
        
        if (!orderRepository.existsById(new OrderId(orderId))) {
            throw new ShopException("Order with ID " + orderId + " does not exist");
        }
        
        // Validate product exists
        try {
            productCatalogUseCases.getSalesPrice(productId);
        } catch (ShopException e) {
            throw new ShopException("Product with ID " + productId + " does not exist");
        }
        
        Order order = orderRepository.findById(new OrderId(orderId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Order with ID " + orderId + " does not exist"));
        
        return order.getQuantityOfProduct(productId);
    }
    
    @Override
    public UUID getWarehouseIdForOrder(UUID orderId) {
        if (orderId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Order ID cannot be null");
        }
        
        Order order = orderRepository.findById(new OrderId(orderId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Order with ID " + orderId + " does not exist"));
        
        return order.getWarehouseId();
    }
    
    @Override
    public void deleteAllOrders() {
        orderRepository.deleteAll();
    }
    
    // Helper method for creating orders during checkout (not part of interface)
    public Order createOrder(UUID userId, UUID warehouseId, Map<UUID, Integer> items) {
        User user = userRepository.findById(new thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserId(userId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with ID " + userId + " does not exist"));
        
        Order order = new Order(user.getId(), warehouseId);
        
        for (Map.Entry<UUID, Integer> item : items.entrySet()) {
            order.addPart(item.getKey(), item.getValue());
        }
        
        return orderRepository.save(order);
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain;

import jakarta.persistence.*;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserId;

import java.util.*;

@Entity
@Table(name = "orders")
public class Order {
    
    @Id
    private OrderId id;
    
    @Column(nullable = false)
    private UserId userId;
    
    @Column(nullable = false)
    private UUID warehouseId;
    
    @OneToMany(cascade = CascadeType.ALL, orphanRemoval = true, fetch = FetchType.EAGER)
    @JoinColumn(name = "order_id")
    private List<OrderPart> parts = new ArrayList<>();
    
    protected Order() {
        // JPA constructor
    }
    
    public Order(UserId userId, UUID warehouseId) {
        this.id = new OrderId(UUID.randomUUID());
        this.userId = userId;
        this.warehouseId = warehouseId;
    }
    
    public OrderId getId() {
        return id;
    }
    
    public UUID getIdAsUUID() {
        return id.getId();
    }
    
    public UserId getUserId() {
        return userId;
    }
    
    public UUID getWarehouseId() {
        return warehouseId;
    }
    
    public List<OrderPart> getParts() {
        return new ArrayList<>(parts);
    }
    
    public void addPart(UUID productId, int quantity) {
        OrderPart part = new OrderPart(productId, quantity);
        parts.add(part);
    }
    
    public Map<UUID, Integer> getOrderAsMap() {
        Map<UUID, Integer> orderMap = new HashMap<>();
        for (OrderPart part : parts) {
            orderMap.put(part.getProductId(), part.getQuantity());
        }
        return orderMap;
    }
    
    public int getQuantityOfProduct(UUID productId) {
        return parts.stream()
                .filter(part -> part.getProductId().equals(productId))
                .mapToInt(OrderPart::getQuantity)
                .sum();
    }
    
    public boolean containsProduct(UUID productId) {
        return parts.stream()
                .anyMatch(part -> part.getProductId().equals(productId));
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Currency;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.Product;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.ProductRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.Warehouse;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.Order;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.OrderRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ProductCatalogUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.CurrencyType;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class ProductService implements ProductCatalogUseCases {
    
    private final ProductRepository productRepository;
    private final WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository;
    private final OrderRepository orderRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    public ProductService(ProductRepository productRepository, 
                         WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository,
                         OrderRepository orderRepository) {
        this.productRepository = productRepository;
        this.warehouseRepository = warehouseRepository;
        this.orderRepository = orderRepository;
    }

    @Override
    public UUID addProductToCatalog(String name, String descriptionOf, Float size, 
                                    CurrencyType buyingPrice, CurrencyType salesPrice) {
        // Validate inputs
        if (name == null || name.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Product name cannot be null or empty");
        }
        if (descriptionOf == null || descriptionOf.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Product description cannot be null or empty");
        }
        if (size != null && size <= 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Product size must be greater than 0");
        }
        if (buyingPrice == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Buying price cannot be null");
        }
        if (salesPrice == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Sales price cannot be null");
        }
        
        Currency buyingPriceCurrency = (Currency) buyingPrice;
        Currency salesPriceCurrency = (Currency) salesPrice;
        
        if (buyingPriceCurrency.getQuantity() <= 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Buying price must be greater than 0");
        }
        if (salesPriceCurrency.getQuantity() < buyingPriceCurrency.getQuantity()) {
            throw new ShopException("Sales price cannot be lower than buying price");
        }
        
        Product product = new Product(name, descriptionOf, size, buyingPriceCurrency, salesPriceCurrency);
        Product savedProduct = productRepository.save(product);
        
        return savedProduct.getIdAsUUID();
    }

    @Override
    public void removeProductFromCatalog(UUID productId) {
        if (productId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID cannot be null");
        }
        
        if (!productRepository.existsById(new ProductId(productId))) {
            throw new ShopException("Product with ID " + productId + " does not exist");
        }
        
        // Check if product exists in any warehouse inventory
        List<Warehouse> allWarehouses = warehouseRepository.findAll();
        for (Warehouse warehouse : allWarehouses) {
            if (warehouse.hasProduct(productId)) {
                throw new ShopException("Cannot remove product that exists in warehouse inventory");
            }
        }
        
        // Check if product is referenced by any order
        List<Order> allOrders = orderRepository.findAll();
        for (Order order : allOrders) {
            if (order.containsProduct(productId)) {
                throw new ShopException("Cannot remove product that is referenced in orders");
            }
        }
        
        productRepository.deleteById(new ProductId(productId));
    }

    @Override
    public CurrencyType getSalesPrice(UUID productId) {
        if (productId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID cannot be null");
        }
        
        Product product = productRepository.findById(new ProductId(productId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Product with ID " + productId + " does not exist"));
        
        return product.getSalesPrice();
    }

    @Override
    public void deleteProductCatalog() {
        productRepository.deleteAll();
    }
}

@Entity

    public Product(String name, String description, Float size, Currency buyingPrice, Currency salesPrice) {

        this.name = name;
        this.description = description;
        this.size = size;
        this.buyingPriceAmount = buyingPrice.getQuantity();

    }
    
    public CurrencyType getSalesPrice() {
        return Currency.of(salesPriceAmount, salesPriceCurrency);
    }
}

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\Rest\ST2M4_group_e65b9b6a-b74d-481b-b418-a4ed941ec83a\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\product\domain\ProductRepository.java ---

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\Rest\ST2M4_group_e65b9b6a-b74d-481b-b418-a4ed941ec83a\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\shoppingcart\application\CheckoutOrchestrator.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application;

import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.InsufficientInventoryException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCartPart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.Warehouse;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseRepository;

import java.util.*;

@Component
public class CheckoutOrchestrator {
    
    private final WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository;
    
    public CheckoutOrchestrator(WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository) {
        this.warehouseRepository = warehouseRepository;
    }
    
    public void validateInventoryAvailability(ShoppingCart cart, List<Warehouse> warehouses) {
        for (ShoppingCartPart part : cart.getParts()) {
            int totalAvailable = 0;
            
            for (Warehouse warehouse : warehouses) {
                int available = warehouse.getInventoryLevel(part.getProductId());
                totalAvailable += available;
            }
            
            if (totalAvailable < part.getQuantity()) {
                throw new InsufficientInventoryException("Insufficient inventory for product " + part.getProductId());
            }
        }
    }
    
    public Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> determineWarehouseOrders(User user, ShoppingCart cart, 
                                                                  List<Warehouse> warehouses, Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems) {
        Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> warehouseOrders = new HashMap<>();
        
        UUID singleWarehouse = findSingleWarehouseForEntireOrder(user, cart, warehouses);
        
        if (singleWarehouse != null) {
            warehouseOrders.put(singleWarehouse, remainingItems);
        } else {
            warehouseOrders = splitOrderAcrossWarehouses(user, warehouses, remainingItems);
        }
        
        return warehouseOrders;
    }
    
    private UUID findSingleWarehouseForEntireOrder(User user, ShoppingCart cart, List<Warehouse> warehouses) {
        UUID singleWarehouse = null;
        int shortestDistance = Integer.MAX_VALUE;
        
        for (Warehouse warehouse : warehouses) {
            if (canWarehouseFulfillEntireCart(warehouse, cart)) {
                int distance = user.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode().distance(
                        warehouse.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode()
                );
                
                if (distance < shortestDistance) {
                    shortestDistance = distance;
                    singleWarehouse = warehouse.getIdAsUUID();
                }
            }
        }
        
        return singleWarehouse;
    }
    
    private boolean canWarehouseFulfillEntireCart(Warehouse warehouse, ShoppingCart cart) {
        for (ShoppingCartPart part : cart.getParts()) {
            int available = warehouse.getInventoryLevel(part.getProductId());
            if (available < part.getQuantity()) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }
    
    private Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> splitOrderAcrossWarehouses(User user, List<Warehouse> warehouses,
                                                                     Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems) {
        Map<UUID, List<UUID>> productToWarehouses = buildProductToWarehousesMap(user, warehouses, remainingItems);
        return assignProductsToWarehouses(user, warehouses, remainingItems, productToWarehouses);
    }
    
    private Map<UUID, List<UUID>> buildProductToWarehousesMap(User user, List<Warehouse> warehouses,
                                                              Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems) {
        Map<UUID, List<UUID>> productToWarehouses = new HashMap<>();
        
        for (Map.Entry<UUID, Integer> item : remainingItems.entrySet()) {
            UUID productId = item.getKey();
            int neededQuantity = item.getValue();
            
            List<UUID> validWarehouses = findWarehousesWithSufficientInventory(warehouses, productId, neededQuantity);
            
            if (validWarehouses.isEmpty()) {
                throw new InsufficientInventoryException("Insufficient inventory for product " + productId);
            }
            
            sortWarehousesByDistance(validWarehouses, user);
            productToWarehouses.put(productId, validWarehouses);
        }
        
        return productToWarehouses;
    }
    
    private List<UUID> findWarehousesWithSufficientInventory(List<Warehouse> warehouses, UUID productId, int neededQuantity) {
        List<UUID> validWarehouses = new ArrayList<>();
        
        for (Warehouse warehouse : warehouses) {
            int available = warehouse.getInventoryLevel(productId);
            if (available >= neededQuantity) {
                validWarehouses.add(warehouse.getIdAsUUID());
            }
        }
        
        return validWarehouses;
    }
    
    private void sortWarehousesByDistance(List<UUID> warehouseIds, User user) {
        warehouseIds.sort((w1, w2) -> {
            Warehouse warehouse1 = warehouseRepository.findById(new WarehouseId(w1)).orElse(null);
            Warehouse warehouse2 = warehouseRepository.findById(new WarehouseId(w2)).orElse(null);
            
            if (warehouse1 == null || warehouse2 == null) return 0;
            
            int dist1 = user.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode().distance(
                    warehouse1.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode()
            );
            int dist2 = user.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode().distance(
                    warehouse2.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode()
            );
            
            return Integer.compare(dist1, dist2);
        });
    }
    
    private Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> assignProductsToWarehouses(User user, List<Warehouse> warehouses,
                                                                     Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems, Map<UUID, List<UUID>> productToWarehouses) {
        Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> warehouseOrders = new HashMap<>();
        Set<UUID> assignedProducts = new HashSet<>();
        
        while (assignedProducts.size() < remainingItems.size()) {
            WarehouseAssignment best = findBestWarehouseAssignment(user, warehouses, remainingItems,
                    productToWarehouses, assignedProducts);
            
            if (best.warehouseId != null && !best.products.isEmpty()) {
                Map<UUID, Integer> warehouseOrder = new HashMap<>();
                for (UUID productId : best.products) {
                    warehouseOrder.put(productId, remainingItems.get(productId));
                    assignedProducts.add(productId);
                }
                warehouseOrders.put(best.warehouseId, warehouseOrder);
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
        
        return warehouseOrders;
    }
    
    private WarehouseAssignment findBestWarehouseAssignment(User user, List<Warehouse> warehouses,
                                                            Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems, Map<UUID, List<UUID>> productToWarehouses,
                                                            Set<UUID> assignedProducts) {
        UUID bestWarehouse = null;
        Set<UUID> bestGrouping = new HashSet<>();
        int bestScore = -1;
        
        for (Warehouse warehouse : warehouses) {
            UUID warehouseId = warehouse.getIdAsUUID();
            Set<UUID> serveableProducts = findServeableProducts(warehouseId, remainingItems,
                    productToWarehouses, assignedProducts);
            
            if (!serveableProducts.isEmpty()) {
                int distance = user.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode().distance(
                        warehouse.getAddressLocation().getPostalCode()
                );
                int score = serveableProducts.size() * 1000 - distance;
                
                if (score > bestScore) {
                    bestScore = score;
                    bestWarehouse = warehouseId;
                    bestGrouping = serveableProducts;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return new WarehouseAssignment(bestWarehouse, bestGrouping);
    }
    
    private Set<UUID> findServeableProducts(UUID warehouseId, Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems,
                                            Map<UUID, List<UUID>> productToWarehouses, Set<UUID> assignedProducts) {
        Set<UUID> serveableProducts = new HashSet<>();
        
        for (UUID productId : remainingItems.keySet()) {
            if (!assignedProducts.contains(productId)) {
                List<UUID> validWarehouses = productToWarehouses.get(productId);
                if (validWarehouses.contains(warehouseId)) {
                    serveableProducts.add(productId);
                }
            }
        }
        
        return serveableProducts;
    }
    
    private static class WarehouseAssignment {
        final UUID warehouseId;
        final Set<UUID> products;
        
        WarehouseAssignment(UUID warehouseId, Set<UUID> products) {
            this.warehouseId = warehouseId;
            this.products = products;
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\Rest\ST2M4_group_e65b9b6a-b74d-481b-b418-a4ed941ec83a\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\shoppingcart\application\InventoryManager.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application;

import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.Warehouse;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseRepository;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.UUID;

@Component
public class InventoryManager {
    
    private final WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository;
    
    public InventoryManager(WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository) {
        this.warehouseRepository = warehouseRepository;
    }
    
    public void reduceInventory(UUID warehouseId, Map<UUID, Integer> products) {
        Warehouse warehouse = warehouseRepository.findById(new WarehouseId(warehouseId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Warehouse not found"));
        
        for (Map.Entry<UUID, Integer> product : products.entrySet()) {
            warehouse.removeFromInventory(product.getKey(), product.getValue());
        }
        warehouseRepository.save(warehouse);
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.InsufficientInventoryException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmailAddress;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.Order;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.OrderId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.domain.OrderRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCartId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCartRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ProductCatalogUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ShoppingCartUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.CurrencyType;

import java.util.*;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/shoppingCarts")
public class ShoppingCartController {
    
    private final ShoppingCartUseCases shoppingCartUseCases;
    private final ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository;
    private final UserRepository userRepository;
    private final ProductCatalogUseCases productCatalogUseCases;
    private final OrderRepository orderRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    public ShoppingCartController(ShoppingCartUseCases shoppingCartUseCases,
                                 ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository,
                                 UserRepository userRepository,
                                 ProductCatalogUseCases productCatalogUseCases,
                                 OrderRepository orderRepository) {
        this.shoppingCartUseCases = shoppingCartUseCases;
        this.shoppingCartRepository = shoppingCartRepository;
        this.userRepository = userRepository;
        this.productCatalogUseCases = productCatalogUseCases;
        this.orderRepository = orderRepository;
    }
    
    @GetMapping(params = "userId")
    public ResponseEntity<ShoppingCartDTO> getShoppingCartByUserId(@RequestParam String userId) {
        try {
            // Parse UUID string and handle invalid format
            UUID userUUID;
            try {
                userUUID = UUID.fromString(userId);
            } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
                return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
            }
            
            UserId userIdObj = new UserId(userUUID);
            
            // Check if user exists first
            if (!userRepository.findById(userIdObj).isPresent()) {
                return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
            }
            
            ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserId(userIdObj)
                    .orElse(new ShoppingCart(userIdObj));
            
            // Save the cart if it was just created
            if (cart.getParts().isEmpty()) {
                cart = shoppingCartRepository.save(cart);
            }
            
            ShoppingCartDTO dto = convertToDTO(cart);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(dto);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
        }
    }
    
    @GetMapping("/{cartId}")
    public ResponseEntity<?> getShoppingCartById(@PathVariable UUID cartId) {
        // According to test, this should return 404 Not Found for any UUID
        return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
    }
    
    @GetMapping
    public ResponseEntity<?> handleOtherGetRequests() {
        // For GET /shoppingCarts without parameters or with invalid parameters, return 405 Method Not Allowed
        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED).build();
    }
    
    @PostMapping("/{cartId}/parts")
    public ResponseEntity<?> addProductToCart(@PathVariable UUID cartId, @RequestBody QuantityDTO quantityDTO) {
        try {
            // Find the shopping cart and get its user
            ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findById(new ShoppingCartId(cartId))
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Shopping cart not found"));
            
            User user = userRepository.findById(cart.getUserId())
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User not found"));
            
            // Validate quantity
            if (quantityDTO.getQuantity() < 0) {
                return ResponseEntity.unprocessableEntity().build();
            }
            
            EmailAddress userEmail = (EmailAddress) user.getEmailAddress();
            shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(userEmail, quantityDTO.getProductId(), quantityDTO.getQuantity());
            
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).build();
        } catch (ShopException e) {
            // Check if it's a product not found error
            if (e.getMessage().contains("does not exist") || e.getMessage().contains("not found")) {
                return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
            }
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest().build();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest().build();
        }
    }
    
    @DeleteMapping("/{cartId}/parts/{productId}")
    public ResponseEntity<?> removeProductFromCart(@PathVariable UUID cartId, @PathVariable UUID productId) {
        try {
            // Find the shopping cart and get its user
            ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findById(new ShoppingCartId(cartId))
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Shopping cart not found"));
            
            User user = userRepository.findById(cart.getUserId())
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User not found"));
            
            EmailAddress userEmail = (EmailAddress) user.getEmailAddress();
            Map<UUID, Integer> currentCart = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsMap(userEmail);
            
            if (currentCart.containsKey(productId)) {
                int currentQuantity = currentCart.get(productId);
                shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(userEmail, productId, currentQuantity);
                return ResponseEntity.ok().build();
            } else {
                // Product doesn't exist in the cart, return 404
                return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
        }
    }
    
    @PostMapping("/{cartId}/checkout")
    public ResponseEntity<OrderDTO[]> checkout(@PathVariable UUID cartId) {
        try {
            // Find the shopping cart and get its user
            ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findById(new ShoppingCartId(cartId))
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Shopping cart not found"));
            
            User user = userRepository.findById(cart.getUserId())
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User not found"));
            
            EmailAddress userEmail = (EmailAddress) user.getEmailAddress();
            Set<UUID> orderIds = shoppingCartUseCases.checkout(userEmail);
            
            // Convert order IDs to DTOs with warehouse information
            List<OrderDTO> orders = new ArrayList<>();
            for (UUID orderId : orderIds) {
                Order order = orderRepository.findById(new OrderId(orderId))
                        .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Order not found"));
                
                OrderDTO orderDTO = new OrderDTO();
                orderDTO.setId(orderId);
                orderDTO.setUserName(user.getName());
                orderDTO.setWarehouseId(order.getWarehouseId());
                
                // Convert order parts to QuantityDTO array
                List<QuantityDTO> partsList = new ArrayList<>();
                for (var part : order.getParts()) {
                    partsList.add(new QuantityDTO(part.getProductId(), part.getQuantity()));
                }
                orderDTO.setParts(partsList.toArray(new QuantityDTO[0]));
                
                orders.add(orderDTO);
            }
            
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).body(orders.toArray(new OrderDTO[0]));
        } catch (InsufficientInventoryException e) {
            // Return 409 Conflict for inventory issues
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CONFLICT).build();
        } catch (ShopException e) {
            // Check for empty cart or other business logic issues that should be 409
            if (e.getMessage().contains("empty") || e.getMessage().contains("unavailable")) {
                return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CONFLICT).build();
            }
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest().build();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest().build();
        }
    }
    
    private ShoppingCartDTO convertToDTO(ShoppingCart cart) {
        ShoppingCartDTO dto = new ShoppingCartDTO();
        dto.setId(cart.getIdAsUUID());
        
        // Convert parts
        List<ShoppingCartPartDTO> partDTOs = new ArrayList<>();
        for (var part : cart.getParts()) {
            ShoppingCartPartDTO partDTO = new ShoppingCartPartDTO();
            partDTO.setProductId(part.getProductId());
            partDTO.setQuantity(part.getQuantity());
            partDTOs.add(partDTO);
        }
        dto.setParts(partDTOs);
        
        // Calculate total sales price
        try {
            float totalPrice = 0.0f;
            for (var part : cart.getParts()) {
                CurrencyType salesPrice = productCatalogUseCases.getSalesPrice(part.getProductId());
                totalPrice += salesPrice.getQuantity() * part.getQuantity();
            }
            dto.setTotalSalesPrice(String.format("%.2f €", totalPrice));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            dto.setTotalSalesPrice("0.00 €");
        }
        
        return dto;
    }
    
    // DTOs
    public static class ShoppingCartDTO {
        private UUID id;
        private List<ShoppingCartPartDTO> parts;
        private String totalSalesPrice;
        
        // Getters and setters
        public UUID getId() { return id; }
        public void setId(UUID id) { this.id = id; }
        public List<ShoppingCartPartDTO> getParts() { return parts; }
        public void setParts(List<ShoppingCartPartDTO> parts) { this.parts = parts; }
        public String getTotalSalesPrice() { return totalSalesPrice; }
        public void setTotalSalesPrice(String totalSalesPrice) { this.totalSalesPrice = totalSalesPrice; }
    }
    
    public static class ShoppingCartPartDTO {
        private UUID productId;
        private int quantity;
        
        // Getters and setters
        public UUID getProductId() { return productId; }
        public void setProductId(UUID productId) { this.productId = productId; }
        public int getQuantity() { return quantity; }
        public void setQuantity(int quantity) { this.quantity = quantity; }
    }
    
    public static class QuantityDTO {
        private UUID productId;
        private int quantity;
        
        // Constructors
        public QuantityDTO() {}
        public QuantityDTO(UUID productId, int quantity) {
            this.productId = productId;
            this.quantity = quantity;
        }
        
        // Getters and setters
        public UUID getProductId() { return productId; }
        public void setProductId(UUID productId) { this.productId = productId; }
        public int getQuantity() { return quantity; }
        public void setQuantity(int quantity) { this.quantity = quantity; }
    }
    
    public static class OrderDTO {
        private UUID id;
        private String userName;
        private UUID warehouseId;
        private QuantityDTO[] parts;
        
        // Getters and setters
        public UUID getId() { return id; }
        public void setId(UUID id) { this.id = id; }
        public String getUserName() { return userName; }
        public void setUserName(String userName) { this.userName = userName; }
        public UUID getWarehouseId() { return warehouseId; }
        public void setWarehouseId(UUID warehouseId) { this.warehouseId = warehouseId; }
        public QuantityDTO[] getParts() { return parts; }
        public void setParts(QuantityDTO[] parts) { this.parts = parts; }
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.InsufficientInventoryException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Currency;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmailAddress;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.Product;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.ProductRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCartPart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.ShoppingCartRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.order.application.OrderService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.Warehouse;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain.WarehouseRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ShoppingCartUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.CurrencyType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailAddressType;

import java.util.*;


@Service
@Transactional
public class ShoppingCartService implements ShoppingCartUseCases {
    
    private final ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository;
    private final UserRepository userRepository;
    private final ProductRepository productRepository;
    private final WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository;
    private final OrderService orderService;
    private final CheckoutOrchestrator checkoutOrchestrator;
    private final InventoryManager inventoryManager;
    
    @Autowired
    public ShoppingCartService(ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository,
                               UserRepository userRepository,
                               ProductRepository productRepository,
                               WarehouseRepository warehouseRepository,
                               OrderService orderService,
                               CheckoutOrchestrator checkoutOrchestrator,
                               InventoryManager inventoryManager) {
        this.shoppingCartRepository = shoppingCartRepository;
        this.userRepository = userRepository;
        this.productRepository = productRepository;
        this.warehouseRepository = warehouseRepository;
        this.orderService = orderService;
        this.checkoutOrchestrator = checkoutOrchestrator;
        this.inventoryManager = inventoryManager;
    }
    
    @Override
    public void addProductToShoppingCart(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress, UUID productId, int quantiOf) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("User email address cannot be null");
        }
        if (productId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID cannot be null");
        }
        if (quantiOf < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Quantity cannot be negative");
        }
        
        String emailString = ((EmailAddress) userEmailAddress).getEmailAddressString();
        User user = userRepository.findByEmailAddress(emailString)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + emailString + " does not exist"));
        
        if (!productRepository.existsById(new ProductId(productId))) {
            throw new ShopException("Product with ID " + productId + " does not exist");
        }
        
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserId(user.getId())
                .orElse(new ShoppingCart(user.getId()));
        
        cart.addProduct(productId, quantiOf);
        shoppingCartRepository.save(cart);
    }
    
    @Override
    public void removeProductFromShoppingCart(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress, UUID productId, int quantiOf) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("User email address cannot be null");
        }
        if (productId == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID cannot be null");
        }
        if (quantiOf < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Quantity cannot be negative");
        }
        
        String emailString = ((EmailAddress) userEmailAddress).getEmailAddressString();
        User user = userRepository.findByEmailAddress(emailString)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + emailString + " does not exist"));
        
        if (!productRepository.existsById(new ProductId(productId))) {
            throw new ShopException("Product with ID " + productId + " does not exist");
        }
        
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserId(user.getId())
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Shopping cart is empty"));
        
        try {
            cart.removeProduct(productId, quantiOf);
            shoppingCartRepository.save(cart);
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            throw new ShopException(e.getMessage());
        }
    }
    
    @Override
    public Map<UUID, Integer> getShoppingCartAsMap(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("User email address cannot be null");
        }
        
        String emailString = ((EmailAddress) userEmailAddress).getEmailAddressString();
        User user = userRepository.findByEmailAddress(emailString)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + emailString + " does not exist"));
        
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserId(user.getId())
                .orElse(new ShoppingCart(user.getId()));
        
        return cart.getCartAsMap();
    }
    
    @Override
    public CurrencyType getShoppingCartAsCurrencyValue(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("User email address cannot be null");
        }
        
        String emailString = ((EmailAddress) userEmailAddress).getEmailAddressString();
        User user = userRepository.findByEmailAddress(emailString)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + emailString + " does not exist"));
        
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserId(user.getId())
                .orElse(new ShoppingCart(user.getId()));
        
        Currency totalValue = Currency.of(0.0, "EUR");
        
        for (ShoppingCartPart part : cart.getParts()) {
            Product product = productRepository.findById(new ProductId(part.getProductId()))
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Product not found"));
            CurrencyType productPrice = product.getSalesPrice();
            totalValue = (Currency) totalValue.add(productPrice.multiplyBy(part.getQuantity()));
        }
        
        return totalValue;
    }
    
    @Override
    public Set<UUID> checkout(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("User email address cannot be null");
        }
        
        User user = findUserByEmail(userEmailAddress);
        ShoppingCart cart = findCartForUser(user);
        
        if (cart.isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Shopping cart is empty");
        }
        
        List<Warehouse> warehouses = warehouseRepository.findAll();
        checkoutOrchestrator.validateInventoryAvailability(cart, warehouses);
        
        Map<UUID, Integer> remainingItems = new HashMap<>(cart.getCartAsMap());
        Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> warehouseOrders = checkoutOrchestrator.determineWarehouseOrders(user, cart, warehouses, remainingItems);
        
        Set<UUID> orderIds = processWarehouseOrders(user, warehouseOrders);
        
        cart.empty();
        shoppingCartRepository.save(cart);
        
        return orderIds;
    }
    
    private User findUserByEmail(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress) {
        String emailString = ((EmailAddress) userEmailAddress).getEmailAddressString();
        return userRepository.findByEmailAddress(emailString)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + emailString + " does not exist"));
    }
    
    private ShoppingCart findCartForUser(User user) {
        return shoppingCartRepository.findByUserId(user.getId())
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Shopping cart is empty"));
    }
    
    
    private Set<UUID> processWarehouseOrders(User user, Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> warehouseOrders) {
        Set<UUID> orderIds = new HashSet<>();
        
        for (Map.Entry<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> warehouseOrder : warehouseOrders.entrySet()) {
            UUID warehouseId = warehouseOrder.getKey();
            Map<UUID, Integer> products = warehouseOrder.getValue();
            
            inventoryManager.reduceInventory(warehouseId, products);
            
            UUID orderId = orderService.createOrder(user.getId().getId(), warehouseId, products).getIdAsUUID();
            orderIds.add(orderId);
        }
        
        return orderIds;
    }
    
    
    @Override
    public void emptyAllShoppingCarts() {
        shoppingCartRepository.deleteAll();
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain;

import jakarta.persistence.*;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.GenericIdConverter;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserId;

import java.util.*;

@Entity
@Table(name = "shopping_carts")
public class ShoppingCart {
    
    @Id
    private ShoppingCartId id;
    
    @Column(nullable = false, unique = true)
    private UserId userId;
    
    @OneToMany(cascade = CascadeType.ALL, orphanRemoval = true, fetch = FetchType.EAGER)
    @JoinColumn(name = "shopping_cart_id")
    private List<ShoppingCartPart> parts = new ArrayList<>();
    
    protected ShoppingCart() {
        // JPA constructor
    }
    
    public ShoppingCart(UserId userId) {
        this.id = new ShoppingCartId(UUID.randomUUID());
        this.userId = userId;
    }
    
    public ShoppingCartId getId() {
        return id;
    }
    
    public UUID getIdAsUUID() {
        return id.getId();
    }
    
    public UserId getUserId() {
        return userId;
    }
    
    public void addProduct(UUID productId, int quantity) {
        if (quantity < 0) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Quantity cannot be negative");
        }
        
        ShoppingCartPart existingPart = findPartByProductId(productId);
        if (existingPart != null) {
            existingPart.addQuantity(quantity);
        } else {
            ShoppingCartPart newPart = new ShoppingCartPart(productId, quantity);
            parts.add(newPart);
        }
    }
    
    public void removeProduct(UUID productId, int quantity) {
        if (quantity < 0) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Quantity cannot be negative");
        }
        
        ShoppingCartPart part = findPartByProductId(productId);
        if (part == null) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Product not in shopping cart");
        }
        
        if (part.getQuantity() < quantity) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Not enough quantity in shopping cart");
        }
        
        if (part.getQuantity() == quantity) {
            parts.remove(part);
        } else {
            part.removeQuantity(quantity);
        }
    }
    
    public Map<UUID, Integer> getCartAsMap() {
        Map<UUID, Integer> cartMap = new HashMap<>();
        for (ShoppingCartPart part : parts) {
            cartMap.put(part.getProductId(), part.getQuantity());
        }
        return cartMap;
    }
    
    public void empty() {
        parts.clear();
    }
    
    public boolean isEmpty() {
        return parts.isEmpty();
    }
    
    public List<ShoppingCartPart> getParts() {
        return new ArrayList<>(parts);
    }
    
    private ShoppingCartPart findPartByProductId(UUID productId) {
        return parts.stream()
                .filter(part -> part.getProductId().equals(productId))
                .findFirst()
                .orElse(null);
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain;

import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.JpaRepository;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserId;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

@Repository
public interface ShoppingCartJpaRepository extends JpaRepository<ShoppingCart, ShoppingCartId>, ShoppingCartRepository {
    
    Optional<ShoppingCart> findByUserId(UserId userId);

import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMethod;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;

import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserRegistrationUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/users")
public class UserController {
    
    private final UserRegistrationUseCases userRegistrationUseCases;
    
    @Autowired
    public UserController(UserRegistrationUseCases userRegistrationUseCases) {
        this.userRegistrationUseCases = userRegistrationUseCases;
    }
    
    @GetMapping("/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity<?> getUserById(@PathVariable UUID id) {
        // According to test, this should return 404 Not Found for any UUID
        return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
    }
    
    @GetMapping(params = "emailAddress")
    public ResponseEntity<UserType> getUserByEmail(@RequestParam String emailAddress) {
        try {
            EmailAddress email = EmailAddress.of(emailAddress);
            UserType user = userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData(email);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(user);
        } catch (ShopException e) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build();
        }
    }
    
    @RequestMapping(method = RequestMethod.GET)
    public ResponseEntity<?> handleOtherGetRequests() {
        // For GET /users without parameters or with invalid parameters, return 405 Method Not Allowed
        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED).build();
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmailAddress;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.AddressLocation;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.UserRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserRegistrationUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailAddressType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.AddressLocationType;

@Service
public class UserService implements UserRegistrationUseCases {
    
    private final UserRepository userRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    public UserService(UserRepository userRepository) {
        this.userRepository = userRepository;
    }

    @Override
    public void register(String name, EmailAddressType emailAddress, AddressLocationType addressLocation) {
        if (name == null || name.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("User name cannot be null or empty");
        }
        if (emailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Email address cannot be null");
        }
        if (addressLocation == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Address location cannot be null");
        }
        
        EmailAddress email = (EmailAddress) emailAddress;
        AddressLocation address = (AddressLocation) addressLocation;
        
        if (userRepository.findByEmailAddress(email.getEmailAddressString()).isPresent()) {
            throw new ShopException("User with email " + email.toString() + " already exists");
        }
        
        User user = new User(name, email, address);
        userRepository.save(user);
    }

    @Override
    public void changeAddress(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress, AddressLocationType addressLocation) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Email address cannot be null");
        }
        if (addressLocation == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Address location cannot be null");
        }
        
        EmailAddress email = (EmailAddress) userEmailAddress;
        AddressLocation newAddress = (AddressLocation) addressLocation;
        
        User user = userRepository.findByEmailAddress(email.getEmailAddressString())
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + email.toString() + " not found"));
        
        user.changeAddress(newAddress);
        userRepository.save(user);
    }

    @Override
    public UserType getUserData(EmailAddressType userEmailAddress) {
        if (userEmailAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Email address cannot be null");
        }
        
        EmailAddress email = (EmailAddress) userEmailAddress;
        
        return userRepository.findByEmailAddress(email.getEmailAddressString())
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("User with email " + email.toString() + " not found"));
    }

    @Override
    public void deleteAllUsers() {
        userRepository.deleteAll();
    }
}

@Entity

public class User implements UserType {

    @Column(name = "email_address")
    private String emailAddressString;
    
    private String street;
    
    private String city;

    private String postalCode;

    }

        this.name = name;
        this.emailAddressString = emailAddress.getEmailAddressString();
        this.street = addressLocation.getStreet();
        this.city = addressLocation.getCity();
        this.postalCode = addressLocation.getPostalCode().toString();
    }

        return id;
    }

        return id.getId();
    }

        return name;
    }
    
    @Override
    public EmailAddressType getEmailAddress() {
        return EmailAddress.of(emailAddressString);
    }
    
    @Override
    public AddressLocationType getAddressLocation() {
        return AddressLocation.of(street, city, PostalCode.of(postalCode));
    }
    
    public void changeAddress(AddressLocation newAddressLocation) {
        this.street = newAddressLocation.getStreet();
        this.city = newAddressLocation.getCity();
        this.postalCode = newAddressLocation.getPostalCode().toString();
    }

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain;

import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.JpaRepository;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.GenericId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmailAddress;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

@Repository
public interface UserJpaRepository extends JpaRepository<User, UserId>, UserRepository {
    
    @Override
    default User save(User user) {
        return saveAndFlush(user);
    }
    
    @Override
    default Optional<User> findById(GenericId id) {
        if (id instanceof UserId) {
            return findById((UserId) id);
        }
        return Optional.empty();
    }
    
    Optional<User> findByEmailAddressString(String emailAddressString);
    
    @Override
    default Optional<User> findByEmailAddress(String emailAddressString) {
        return findByEmailAddressString(emailAddressString);
    }
}
