                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                        userEmailAddress0, productId1, 4 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                        userEmailAddress0, productId2, 5 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testAddRemoveProductsFromAndToShoppingCart() {
        // given
        UUID productId1 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 1 );
        UUID productId2 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 2 );
        EmailAddressType userEmailAddress3 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmailAddress( 3 );
        EmailAddressType userEmailAddress5 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmailAddress( 5 );

        // when user 3 ...
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress3, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress3, productId2, 3 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress3, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress3, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress3, productId2, 6 );
        Map<UUID, Integer> cart3 = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsMap( userEmailAddress3 );
        // user3 has 1x productId1 and 9x productId2 in cart

        // ... and when user 5 ...
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress5, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress5, productId2, 8 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress5, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress5, productId2, 2 );
        Map<UUID, Integer> cart5 = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsMap( userEmailAddress5 );
        // user5 has 1x productId1 and 10x productId2 in cart

        // then
        assertEquals( 2, cart3.size() );
        assertEquals( 1, cart3.get( productId1 ) );
        assertEquals( 9, cart3.get( productId2 ) );

        assertEquals( 2, cart5.size() );
        assertEquals( 1, cart5.get( productId1 ) );
        assertEquals( 10, cart5.get( productId2 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testShoppingCartValue() {
        // given
        UUID productId3 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 3 );
        UUID productId6 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 6 );
        UUID productId8 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 8 );
        CurrencyType price3 = productTestHelper.getSalesPrice( 3 );
        CurrencyType price6 = productTestHelper.getSalesPrice( 6 );
        CurrencyType price8 = productTestHelper.getSalesPrice( 8 );
        EmailAddressType userEmailAddress3 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmailAddress( 3 );

        // when
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart( userEmailAddress3, productId3, 3 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart( userEmailAddress3, productId6, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart( userEmailAddress3, productId8, 5 );
        // user3 has 3x productId3, 2x productId6 and 5x productId8 in cart
        CurrencyType cartValue = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsCurrencyValue( userEmailAddress3 );

        // then
        assertEquals( price3.multiplyBy( 3 ).add( price6.multiplyBy( 2 ) ).add( price8.multiplyBy( 5 ) ),
                cartValue );
    }

    @Test
    public void testUnsuccessfulCheckout() {
        // given user buying product 0 (which is not in inventory), and user 1 buying product 1
        // in a bigger quantity (11) than available (10)
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        EmailAddressType userEmailAddress0 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmailAddress( 0 );
        EmailAddressType userEmailAddress1 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmailAddress( 1 );
        UUID productId0 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 0 );
        UUID productId1 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 1 );

        // when
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress0, productId0, 1 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmailAddress1, productId1, 11 );

        // then
        assertThrows( InsufficientInventoryException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.checkout( userEmailAddress0 ) );
        assertThrows( InsufficientInventoryException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.checkout( userEmailAddress1 ) );
    }

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.testtests;

import com.tngtech.archunit.core.domain.JavaClass;
import com.tngtech.archunit.core.domain.JavaClasses;
import com.tngtech.archunit.core.domain.JavaMethod;
import com.tngtech.archunit.core.importer.ClassFileImporter;
import com.tngtech.archunit.lang.ArchRule;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.helpers.ShoppingCartRESTHelper;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.owntests.DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.owntests.OwnShoppingCartRESTTest;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.CurrencyType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailAddressType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PostalCodeType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.AddressLocationType;

import static com.tngtech.archunit.lang.syntax.ArchRuleDefinition.classes;
import static org.springframework.test.util.AssertionErrors.assertTrue;

/**
 * This test checks if there are the appropriate tests in the test class(es) for domain
 * primitives.
 */

public class RulesForOwnTests {
    private JavaClass dpTestClass, restTestClass;
    private JavaClasses dpTestClasses, restTestClasses;
    private static final String WAREHOUSE_DOMAIN_PACKAGE =
            "thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.warehouse.domain";
    private static final String WAREHOUSE_CLASS_NAME =
            WAREHOUSE_DOMAIN_PACKAGE + ".Warehouse";


    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() throws Exception {
        dpTestClass = new ClassFileImporter().importClass( DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest.class );
        restTestClass = new ClassFileImporter().importClass( OwnShoppingCartRESTTest.class );

        dpTestClasses = new ClassFileImporter().importClasses( DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest.class );
        restTestClasses = new ClassFileImporter().importClasses( OwnShoppingCartRESTTest.class );
    }


    @Test
    public void ensureMinimumNumberOfTestMethods() {
        // given
        // when
        int dpTestMethodCount = getTestMethodCount( dpTestClass );
        int restTestMethodCount = getTestMethodCount( restTestClass );

        // then
        assertTrue( "There should be at least 4 test methods in the dp test class, but there are only "
                        + dpTestMethodCount,dpTestMethodCount >= 2 );
        assertTrue( "There should be at least 5 test methods in the rest test class, but there are only "
                        + restTestMethodCount, restTestMethodCount >= 5 );
    }

    private int getTestMethodCount( JavaClass testClass ) {
        int testMethodCount = 0;
        for ( JavaMethod method : testClass.getMethods() ) {
            if ( isTestMethod( method ) ) {
                testMethodCount++;
            }
        }
        return testMethodCount;
    }

    private boolean isTestMethod( JavaMethod method ) {
        return method.isAnnotatedWith( Test.class );
    }


    @Test
    public void dpTestsShouldReferenceTheRightClasses() {
        ArchRule rule = classes()
                .should().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( PostalCodeType.class )
                .andShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( CurrencyType.class )
                .andShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( AddressLocationType.class )
                .andShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( EmailAddressType.class )
                .because( "DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest should reference PostalCode, " +
                        "Currency, EmailAddress, and AddressLocation!" );
        rule.check( dpTestClasses );
    }


    @Test
    public void restTestsShouldReferenceEmailAddress() {
        ArchRule rule = classes()
                .should().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( EmailAddressType.class )
                .because( "WarehouseComparatorUnitTest should reference EmailAddressType!" );
        rule.check( restTestClasses );
    }


    @Test
    public void restTestsShouldReferenceRESTControllers() {
        ArchRule rule = classes()
                .should().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAnnotatedWith( RestController.class )
                .orShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( ShoppingCartRESTHelper.class )
                .because( "WarehouseComparatorUnitTest should call REST controllers! " +
                        "(either directly or via the ShoppingCartRESTHelper REST helper)" );
        rule.check( restTestClasses );
    }

}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.user;

import jakarta.transaction.Transactional;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.boot.test.autoconfigure.web.servlet.AutoConfigureMockMvc;
import org.springframework.boot.test.context.SpringBootTest;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Import;
import org.springframework.test.web.servlet.MockMvc;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.helpers.impl.RESTTestHelperConfiguration;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserRegistrationUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailAddressType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.AddressLocationType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.*;

import java.util.UUID;

import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.request.MockMvcRequestBuilders.get;
import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.result.MockMvcResultMatchers.jsonPath;
import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.result.MockMvcResultMatchers.status;

@SpringBootTest
@Transactional
@AutoConfigureMockMvc
@Import( RESTTestHelperConfiguration.class )
public class UserRESTTest {
    @Autowired
    private UserRegistrationUseCases userRegistrationUseCases;
    @Autowired
    private Purgatory purgatory;
    @Autowired
    private UserTestHelper userTestHelper;
    @Autowired
    private MockMvc mockMvc;

    private UUID randomId;
    private EmailAddressType nonExistingEmailAddress;

    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() {
        purgatory.deleteEverything();
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();

        nonExistingEmailAddress = FactoryMethodInvoker.instantiateEmailAddress(
                "harry@sally.de" );
        randomId = UUID.randomUUID();
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidUserUris() throws Exception {
        // given
        String allUsersUri = "/users";
        String randomIdUri = "/users/" +  randomId;
        String nonExistingEmailAddressUri = "/users?emailAddress=" + nonExistingEmailAddress;
        String randomParamUri = "/users?randomParam=randomValue";

        // when
        // then
        mockMvc.perform( get( allUsersUri ) ).andExpect( status().isMethodNotAllowed() );
        mockMvc.perform( get( randomIdUri ) ).andExpect( status().isNotFound() );
        mockMvc.perform( get( nonExistingEmailAddressUri ) ).andExpect( status().isNotFound() );
        mockMvc.perform( get( randomParamUri ) ).andExpect( status().is4xxClientError() );
    }


    @Test
    public void testRandomUserId() throws Exception {
        // given
        String invalidUri = "/users/" +  randomId;

        // when
        // then
        mockMvc.perform( get( invalidUri ) ).andExpect( status().isNotFound() );
    }


    @Test
    public void testQueryUser() throws Exception {
        // given
        EmailAddressType emailAddress4 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmailAddress( 4 );
        String userUri4 = "/users?emailAddress=" + emailAddress4;

        // when
        UserType user4 = userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData( emailAddress4 );
        String name = userTestHelper.getUserName( 4 );
        AddressLocationType addressLocation4 = userTestHelper.getUserAddressLocation( 4 );

        // then (check using JSONPath)
        mockMvc.perform( get( userUri4 ) )
                .andExpect( status().isOk() )
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$.name" ).value( name ) )
                // id is position 0 (cannot be tested with current API structure), name is position 1,
                // email address is 2, address location is 3)
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$..emailAddressString" ).value( emailAddress4.toString() ) )
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$..city" ).value( addressLocation4.getCity() ) )
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$..postalCodeString" ).value(
                        addressLocation4.getPostalCode().toString() ) );
    }

}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.warehouse;

import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.boot.test.context.SpringBootTest;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.ProductTestHelper;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.WarehouseTestHelper;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.Purgatory;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ProductCatalogUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.WarehouseUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.AddressLocationType;

import java.util.UUID;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;
import static thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.FactoryMethodInvoker.instantiatePostalCode;
import static thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.FactoryMethodInvoker.instantiateAddressLocation;


/**
 * This test checks the management and lifecycle of warehouses.
 */
@SpringBootTest
public class WarehouseManagementTest {
    @Autowired
    private WarehouseUseCases warehouseUseCases;
    @Autowired
    private ProductCatalogUseCases productCatalogUseCases;
    @Autowired
    private Purgatory purgatory;
    @Autowired
    private ProductTestHelper productTestHelper;
    @Autowired
    private WarehouseTestHelper warehouseTestHelper;

    private AddressLocationType someAddressLocation;
    private UUID nonExistingId1;
    private UUID nonExistingId2;


    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() {
        purgatory.deleteEverything();
        productTestHelper.addAllProducts();

        someAddressLocation = instantiateAddressLocation( "Some Street", "Some City",
                instantiatePostalCode( "90001" ) );
        nonExistingId1 = UUID.randomUUID();
        nonExistingId2 = UUID.randomUUID();
    }


    @Test
    public void testAddInvalidWarehouse() {
        // given
        String name = "Lager1";

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addNewWarehouse(
                        null, someAddressLocation ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addNewWarehouse(
                        "", someAddressLocation ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addNewWarehouse(
                        name, null ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testDeleteAllWarehousesWhenEmpty() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( false );
        UUID productId9 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 9 );
        UUID warehouseId1 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 1 );
        UUID warehouseId2 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 2 );

        // when
        int numOf1 = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId1, productId9 );
        int numOf2 = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId2, productId9 );

        // then
        assertEquals( 0, numOf1 );
        assertEquals( 0, numOf2 );
        warehouseUseCases.deleteAllWarehouses();
        // ... ids must be invalid now
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId1, productId9 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId2, productId9 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testDeleteAllWarehousesWhenFull() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID productId7 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 7 );
        UUID warehouseId1 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 1 );
        UUID warehouseId2 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 2 );

        // when
        int numOf1 = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId1, productId7 );
        int numOf2 = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId2, productId7 );

        // then
        assertTrue( numOf1 == 3 );
        assertTrue( numOf2 == 3 );
        warehouseUseCases.deleteAllWarehouses();
        // ... ids must be invalid now
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId1, productId7 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId2, productId7 ) );
    }



    @Test
    public void testAddToInventory() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in warehouse 0
        UUID warehouseId0 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 0 );
        int originalInventory5 =
                warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseInventory( 0, 5 );

        // when
        int inventory5before = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId5 );
        warehouseUseCases.addToInventory( warehouseId0, productId5, 23 );
        int inventory5after = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId5 );
        warehouseUseCases.addToInventory( warehouseId0, productId5, 0 );
        int inventory5after2 = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId5 );

        // then
        assertEquals( originalInventory5, inventory5before );
        assertEquals( inventory5before + 23, inventory5after );
        assertEquals( inventory5after, inventory5after2 );
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidAddToInventory() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID productId2 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 2 );
        UUID warehouseId0 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 0 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addToInventory( nonExistingId1, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addToInventory(
                        warehouseId0, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addToInventory(
                        nonExistingId1, productId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.addToInventory(
                        warehouseId0, productId2, -1 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testRemoveFromInventory() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID warehouseId0 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 0 );
        UUID productId0 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 0 ); // 0 in warehouse 0
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in warehouse 0
        UUID productId6 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 6 ); // random >30 in warehouse 0
        int inventory0before =
                warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseInventory( 0, 0 );
        int inventory5before =
                warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseInventory( 0, 5 );
        int inventory6before =
                warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseInventory( 0, 6 );

        // when
        warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory( warehouseId0, productId5, 1 );
        int inventory5after = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId5 );
        warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory( warehouseId0, productId0, 0 );
        int inventory0after = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId0 );
        warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory(
                warehouseId0, productId6, inventory6before );
        int inventory6after = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId6 );

        // then
        assertEquals( inventory5before - 1, inventory5after );
        assertEquals( inventory0before, inventory0after );
        assertEquals( 0, inventory6after );
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidRemoveFromInventory() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID warehouseId0 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 0 );
        UUID productId0 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 0 ); // 0 in warehouse 0
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in warehouse 0
        int inventory5before =
                warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseInventory( 0, 5 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory( nonExistingId1, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory(
                        warehouseId0, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory(
                        nonExistingId1, productId5, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory(
                        warehouseId0, productId5, -1 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory(
                        warehouseId0, productId5, inventory5before + 1 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> warehouseUseCases.removeFromInventory(
                        warehouseId0, productId0, 1 ) ); // already 0 in warehouse 0
    }


    @Test
    public void testChangeInventory() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID warehouseId0 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 0 );
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in warehouse 0

        // when
        warehouseUseCases.changeInventoryTo( warehouseId0, productId5, 111 );
        int inventory5after = warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory( warehouseId0, productId5 );

        // then
        assertEquals( 111, inventory5after );
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidChangeInventory() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID warehouseId0 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 0 );
        UUID productId6 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 6 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> warehouseUseCases.changeInventoryTo(
                nonExistingId1, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> warehouseUseCases.changeInventoryTo(
                nonExistingId1, productId6, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> warehouseUseCases.changeInventoryTo(
                warehouseId0, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> warehouseUseCases.changeInventoryTo(
                warehouseId0, productId6, -1 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testEmptyWarehouse() {
        // given
        warehouseTestHelper.addAllWarehouses( true );
        UUID warehouseId9 = warehouseTestHelper.getWarehouseId( 9 ); // empty warehouse

        // when
        int totalInventory = 0;
        for ( int iProduct = 0; iProduct < productTestHelper.numberOfProducts(); iProduct++ ) {
            UUID productId = productTestHelper.getProductId( iProduct );
            totalInventory += warehouseUseCases.getAvailableInventory(
                    warehouseId9, productId );
        }

        // then
        assertEquals( 0, totalInventory );
    }



}
